# ========== イベント設定情報ファイル ==========
# ====== Event setup information file ========
#
#
REV          STDx0B
#
# ﾃﾞｰﾀ種別   E  : ｲﾍﾞﾝﾄ
#            R  : ﾚﾎﾟｰﾄ
#
# DataType: E == Collection Event
#           L == List of collection events.
#                For example, see how the events RC1LimitAI0 -- RC1LimitAI63 are defined.
#           R == Report
#
# Event Number: Corresponds to defined constants in HCcuConst.pas
#               For example, Event ID $00011010 corresponds to the constant EV_EQUIPMENT_OFFLINE, 
#
# DetectionState: Appears to be a flag of whether the specific collection event is present or not.
#                 For example, this flag is 0 for LL3 and LL4 events.
#
# ReportState: Appears to be a flag as to whether the event is on by default.
#              This corresponds to the CEED value in the SECS/GEM Manual
#
# Event ID: is the Hex code for the SECS/GEM Event ID (CEID).
#
#ﾃﾞｰﾀ種別  ｲﾍﾞﾝﾄ番号  検出状態  報告状態    ｲﾍﾞﾝﾄID   定義ﾘｽﾄ数
#                                                     定義ﾘｽﾄ
#
# DataType EventNumber DetectionState ReportState EventID(hex) #OfDefinedReports
#                                                               ListOfReportIDs
#
